Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramie is so weak that it comes from the eggs, and this material is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And this moisture does not come from beating on the eggs, and this moisture has many colors: or it is a declining color to yellow, or it is without red, or black, or white water, and such happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs of this assembly, for if it is white sifac which we have mentioned, then it is long in shape, like the figure of an egg, and does not open the joints, because it has moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the cloth itself, then the abscesses are rational with part of the egg, and because of this one thinks that it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	and if the moisture is between the leather of the testicles and the white sac, then it feels warm; so that when you want to know the color of the moisture, try all of the introitus because its form is in front.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	So according to this, who comes after the introitus, judge who is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we cure it with fire, so that the patient is healed according to his power and the repletion of his body; then he lies down on his back, on something a little high, and cover him with drapes.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit down on his left side, and command the minister to sit on the right, and extend the stick to one of the 20 ribs at the end of the loins.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula and peel the skin from among the loins to the tip of the hand until you reach a thin piece of flesh, then cut it carefully, leaving a little bit of the skin on the meat, and parboil it very slightly.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Then pierce the flesh with a large needle, and drain out all the water, then put on your gloves, and draw up the skin. And do not touch the meat with the needle, but only slice it very finely; peel off each piece separately so that you can see well to cut it properly, or the water will come back into it again.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the skin suits you well to your work, then return it to its place when you have finished working on the flesh; and sew together the 20 ribs of meat with one stitch, and wash it as you would the other wounds until it is healthy again.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corruppt by some other disease, it is necessary that you lay the eggs that are suspended, in doubt of corruption of blood; then take the egg and remove it, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if the water is assembled in two parts together, knowing that there are two branches; then take the other part as you did with the first, evenly, and wash the blood, and put in the wound another wet one with oil.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put there another wet one with wine and oil, and put on the two eggs, and cover them with double cloths, and tie it up all together according to this form:
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take 2 cloths, and fill them with wool fabric according to this shape and sew them together in the throat of the shirt, and one of the two shoulders should preigne on the bottom until the back, and the other over the 2 arms, and the other two should be gathered in a loop around the neck;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and there is no time when this medicine of the fire caustic is in place of iron tweezers, and that you squeeze .i. the caustic scraper, and scrape the skin of the coccyx, and it is heated as we have said, so that the white cure that contains the water comes out;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if you take the caustic according to this form, and pierce it as with an awl, and scorch it with this fine fire caustic:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And take the coat in all the ways that you can, until it is completely removed; and be careful that the fire does not touch the uvula; and know that this work is safer; and move with caution to prevent the opening of a vein; and beware of the size of the caustic;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything makes you uncomfortable, or an abscess or a opening of a vein or anything else, then treat what makes you uncomfortable, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the sick person is afraid, and does not want to wait for this work because of its ugliness, then you should make a puncture, as I told you, and it is that when you are sure by the meanings that we have said that the ramose water is there,
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	make the sick person sit up; then pierce the abscess in the middle of the face all the way through, and place the puncture deep into the neck; and make the hole large so that all the water runs out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton in the hole, and tie it up, and leave it to run out the remaining water, then clean it as long as the wound heals;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and if the bleach cotton does not let the water run out in the mouth of the wound, then you should put a pen or instrument used to drain the water from drops into it, so that its shape is as follows; and widen .i. poc the wound, and know that the water returns, and is gathered after 15 days or so, and when it is gathered as before, and in such a way that the sick person's days pass.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the penis from the anus
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	I know that in this chapter about the use of fire, there are many different ways to treat it, so I think it is better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and the appearances of the penis.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say then that many penises come from the corons, and most often from the coions; and this is by much case.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	It is known that by too much acrid and bitter food, which expands to the bowels, or from impact.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And the color of the abscess according to the color of the flesh; and does not test for pain, and is an abscess wound;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And sometimes it is a painful and piercing abscess, and of a foxy color, and never comes from a nerve, or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from a nerve, if it is hot by the position of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it is not necessary for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	Those who are made from the swelling of a vein are known by their tendency to express themselves through the touching of both sides.
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	and one can well make a size on this resemblance, and on the other characters;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and is that you cut the knot of the coins, then the egg in the top, and the trail is firm white milk, and deliver the suspender from all sides of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hard with these new feathers, then it is necessary that you take the egg, and the cup.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is still alive in the shell, or in this one which is inside the vessels, then it is necessary that you deliver all of those held, and the cup rolls.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the feather is behind, then it is necessary that you cop it all, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your wounds are finished, take the wool of sheep wet with oil and wine, then the cure for others as long as they are healthy.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the prostate from the urethra
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an old French text describing a medical procedure:
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	and the patient will be less painful when he goes;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	and the cure for this disease is very good if it is treated with caution as described above;

puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound as you do with other wounds or wound the bowels so that no vessel is left unhealed;

si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the eyes do not lose their vision through the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the syrup
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	of the rupture of the syrup
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	and this wound is where the medicine, or its extension, comes from these 17 causes: or by percussion, or by jump, or by braying, or by lifting a grievous burden, and by similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is an extension of the medicine, if it happens that it comes little by little, for a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the apoplexy is even until almost perfect, so that the medicine hurries the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac. Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And let there be no separation of the small intestine with the colon, for it is held back and causes great pain to the patient, even when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	For in these cures by fire, lest he should be scorched.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of this work is that you command the patient to keep the intestine in his hand inside the wound, if he can go back in;

puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	Then pour in the liquid inside the waistcoat with your index finger, in the middle where the skin is white, and between the two sides of white skin that are exposed;

et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and ask your two assistants if they feel any hard or white matter wrapped around the intestine; and if you find nothing, cut it open.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	then take a needle or thread made of fine wire, and cut it open at the back where the skin is; then sew it up with the thread after the entrails have been removed; then tie off the ends of the thread, so that there are three threads left;

Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And never is cauterized with white of egg that we have said, after the incision, from doubt of decay of blood.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For this often happens, and leaves the thread in place while it is chewing; and if it delays at chewing, so let it be raised with hot water, and put on what we have said, as long as it chews.

de hernie carnouse	of hernia carnous
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this recipe I have never seen anyone try to make a cure for hernias with fire.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the old one said that it is made thus: as you join the threads of a scarf, so tie the straps, lightly at first, on the outside after cutting them very short;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then sew it together, and heal the injury of him who suffers, as we have said, until he is healthy.

et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	and it is that the patient lies still on his back between your hands, then measure the width with two fingers according to the quantity of .ii.

dou chastrement	To cauterize with fire
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	I see that cauterization is mentioned in our law, and for this reason I would like to say nothing about it in this book; and there are only two methods: one is that the fire should be used to respond when asked, and to heal using fire; and the other, because we have often had to use cauterization on certain animals to help us, such as sheep, goats, and others. Therefore, I say that cauterization can be done in 2 ways: either by attraction or by cutting. In the one where we use attraction, we should sit the animal in hot water until the skin is softened and relaxed; then grab it with your hand, until it is healed and you no longer feel it. From the size of the cut: you should burn the animal, and tie the leather from the coals to your left hand, then put on the suspender, and cut each ear at 1 inch, when you have well scarred them; and leave no little bit of skin and fine hair which is under the saddles. And this method of cauterization is milder than the one done by attraction, because by attraction something may remain from the cuts, so that the animal wants to luxuriate, then heal the wound as soon as it is healed.

et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch them evenly by moving one way and the other, so that they come out, and are held in place by teeth, as is shown here:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if one part stops, so grease his two feet with oil, and push it in that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if one point stops, so put this oncine or higher up, and make it as much as it comes out all at once.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and cannot be brought back by the tightness,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it in a sheet, until it is completely dry;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	Then apply the ointment to the joint of the foot or ankle, and in the other hand, do the same for the other leg;
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child is large and is stuck in the birth canal, or has an acute angle,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	If it is necessary for you to press the thorny spittle between your two, and make the head and extract the needle.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you rub it with the instrument which is called "almond", of which the form comes with the instruments or paste which follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And so likewise I make it grow naturally by means of the instrument which is called "almond"; and in this way it grows into a great natural head;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pull out the bones with nails,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the head of the shoulder is cut off and forced out, so that it is split, until the moisture which is outside has gone.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces with a knife.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the abdomen or the sides, so that you pierce it until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	and if it is stuck in its place, then it should be removed gently, and the treatment of the wound should be light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is stuck in the belly or breast, if you think that you will take it out with .i. a cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and making the belly or breast, as much as the moisture which is there;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if the other member has been broken, and the head stays in place,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	so that the hand of the patient is completely freed from the ring, and pulls it out to the mouth of the ring;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then pour in . i. a cup of water, and let it rest.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth is constricted by heat that has come to it, so that it does not work properly
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then provide wet and greasy things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and provide plasters, and cut into acidic, moistening, and soothing substances.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if it has fallen on its chest, and you can make it level, bring what we have said about the live child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one does not have power, then let the man be taken apart piece by piece, and leave nothing of the second.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, bring what we have said about the legs that come out in the mare;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if they come out with blood, so let it be placed in water restricting them, and bring other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman whose womb had taken the life of one child, then consults another on that body, and denies death to the others.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, the apoplexy in the brain burst, and began to cause great disease.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, but I could not stop the wound from bleeding.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on an ointment of strong attraction, and inserted a bone, and after a few days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled much, for there is no bone in his belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I want to heal the wound, and with two hands I will put on the plaster, as long as the woman is in better shape;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and wait for the woman to get well soon, and it was already a little bow at the joint;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter for the sake of that which, when the master tries an odd thing, he may know how to help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the dislocated shoulder to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here comes the form of the pressor, where we put the books; and at two turns to the two shoulders of the two legs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be thinner than the restrector, and made of ebony or boxwood; and they should have a curved shape.
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let his mouth be as big as two hands across, and his cheekbones as wide as a palm.
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and the three pieces of the skin be sewed together from one end to the other, a length of a palm and a half or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two pieces are inserted into the mouth of the mare to open it when the two horns are turned.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, its appearance more subtle and lighter, is made from ebony or boxwood according to the shape of the nails;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and let there be two joints, as you see, of a palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you open the leg with all the instrument, so that the woman sits on one bed, the feet during and the legs open,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then bottle the two joints together in the leg, and hold the head of the instrument between her knees;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then open your hand with all the instrument, as you did with the tweezers evenly, according to the quantity that you opened the mouth of the leg, until the ball moves;
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	All these instruments are mounted upside down, and varied in number according to the work; and when you have prepared them, so much the faster is the operation, and so much the higher are the tools for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not mount the instrument well in advance, because there is no excuse for its necessity.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second is ready for delivery, you must instruct the patient to retain her hair and then make her sneeze by pressing on her nose and mouth.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she sneezes, that is good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, if it is possible, and make a hole or cover, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the wound, so as chamomile, mint, fennel, camomile, camilac and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	all of these herbs, or any of them, are cooked or boiled in water on the fire; then put a tube or cover from the pot, and the other head into the mouth of the wound,
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and let the steam come out into the wound; then make it cough, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If so, take the second immediately.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not healed, order the doctor to soak his left hand in oil of sesame or in a musk of altitude, and then let it dry out in nature,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and wants the second; and when she has found it, if she pinches it and extends it little by little correctly, so that the nail does not come off in extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but then it must be moved lightly from side to side, and then pull it; and it will come out and loosen itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the nail of the finger is bent or broken, we have said the cure for wringing, and for smoke from herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not from all those things we have said, then take care that you do not follow the trail.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is in the mouth of the mare, you bind him to the cunt of the woman, then cauterize with ointment of four-fold power;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if it is not well done and then reset, and will come again with force; but nevertheless, when it is well done, if it is not done with care, then the odour of porridge will go up to the stomach and head, and darken the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	So it is necessary that you make smoke that can be done to it: no one of the ancients has tried smoking with dandelion and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument, let one fume the woman at the retention of flowers and of the second if is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is to see like to a dog, and one puts the head thin in the nature, and the shoulders wide by fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigations on the coals, and the tan until it is wasted, and restart another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who have not yet received the foundation of the jaw, but it is broken with a subtle medicine.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it is necessary that he who has been broken should break the jaw of him who has not yet been broken, and not break his own jaw with the sputum that comes from him, and fasten the bandage so that he does not touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put another moist cloth on it with wine and oil, then treat it with ointment until it is well.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not recover, then put a piece of string around his hand, and let it hang down, and when the child walks, let him move his hand, so that the bone does not stick to the skin.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And there is no sudden shock of a wound or abscess; if it is necessary to cover this sudden shock: if it is to be cured, as we said in the case of the cane of plunking.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	fistulas that come from the root are a disease, and grow worse than those that come from the root in the space of the .ij. parts, or
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is one fistula or more; and when that nodation is old, if it opens, and with cold water or a weak brew, or
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they do not become such fisticules; and they are understood by whom it is or defecation or windiness when the patient has defecation, and by chance in jump one side.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if they are fisticules that pierce only up to the bladder, and only halfway up the shaft; and reach up to the intersection of the thigh, and up to the nose.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus we understand a persisting fisticule at the fundament, and not persisting:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And it is that you stick your little finger or foundation, and stick a fine needle of silver or iron in the fisticule when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is tortuosity, if I put a thin piece of string or .i. horsehair between your teeth so that you can feel the string or hair at the back of your throat;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you don't feel it, and there is no pain or difficulty in swallowing, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	that it does not pierce you; if you hurry to heal it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And if the fistula is persisting up to the bladder or urinary conduit, and if the urine can't be held back with medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is cut just to the join of the cunt, then he must hold it coming up to his loins.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twisting or the pain does not come from within, but rather it has already been bent forward, and there is no medicine or sudden relief by feeling;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persistent fissures there is no cure but toil, and the vain ambition of foolish men who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is neither persistent nor ancient, there is hope for health through fire, as I have experienced, and
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and so the patient lies down between your hands on his back; and he lowers his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs bent towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then pour water on an ash pile, or mud if there is curvature, as long as you can tell where the pile comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	so that the patient's heart is felt at the base of the spine, and if that is difficult, then you put your little finger on it.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	then know that the ash has caught the fire; and whether it is uncovered or not, you feel between your thumb and finger, so you know if it is persistent.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If not treated, they will never heal.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One should treat these in a particular way, but it is difficult to do so well; however, it can be done well with care;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that one gives, if one heats the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as it is said above;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and the bottle is filled hot in the fistula, as far as it comes out smoothly from the base; and make this iij times or iii, until you know that these hairs are burned, which seem to a feather of an owl;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the doctor of tent-cloth immerses it, until that which is soaked comes out, and then the doctor of ointment immerses it while wringing it out, and binding it together.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is so, it is good. If not, then it cannot be made well;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it is placed between, and does not pierce until the top which is at the foundation, and between your two palms place a thick covering of tar or syrup, and you see the fistula to that which is under the covering from the palm's tip;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the cover of the encumbrance of the fistula, and seals before the tent, and then treat after, until it comes to the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and will be delivered the trial, and grief; then cursed are those birds-of-prey that seem a feather of an owl, and none remains without.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the sun does not go out, and a wound between you and the work, if the fire cautery or medicine ague.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cautery assembles .ij. bone things: namely, the burning of those dislocated joints, and the bleeding of blood and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	and then the healing of wet wounds or dry sores, as long as the bones are hot, and those dislocated joints are burned in the fire;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	and then heal the wound with the medicine of dry spices.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For once healed, it is well and never returns worse.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up to the very foundation, and is separated from the heart, it will burst at that place, and inquire about that.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the pain, and go in. iij. is the medicine or charm or balm, where it is ready to pierce, if there is only a way of faith and hope, by the administration of one of the iii. ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	Here is the translation of the text line-by-line into English:
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not over-heat too much, that you do not cover up the foundation which holds the base, and let the dislocations come by natural means;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	In case it is healthy again, or you remove the covering and clean it completely from the base, or with a tool pointed;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	and then my faith, this good tree that is in the wound, as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	and then study to restore the wound, and to delay the fistula in the part further from the fundament: for that is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And no way are there fistulas according to this manner: and it is when you plug the tent in the fistula, and she is or costit doulx cur of lez lu cuir desous,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	if one takes a tent pierced at the top according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And I put in one end of the wire, and pour it into the tent through all the wire at the hole until it comes to the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is persistent in the margin of the foundation inside, then pull out the wire from that hole, so that you pour your two from that foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and tie the end of the wire to the head, and join the 12 ends together, and pull them apart, and leave it 1 hour or 12 hours;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and do not restrain it once, until the wire connects these strings that are between two, and they chafe;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound as long as it is swollen and inflamed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If there is no fistula, then pierce it in all ways that you can, unless it is too completely closed.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it does not suffice to make a ligature if it is completely closed, and then heal it, as we have said, until it is healthy.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spike that you make for the fistula if it is acute, and then you cut;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other hand no, for this you do not cut what you should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	are according to the following manner: they are within the fundament, also as grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and cut them off in place.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and if they are one or more, and are away from the fundament and at the top of the fundament; but those that are away have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and then again when a little water or blood, and has the color of the flesh.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and then again when a little water or blood, and has the color of the flesh. Order the patient to sweat by going to chambers, until the foundations go out, and the seed begins;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, and hold it with your fingernail, then cut it at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot hold them with their moisture, take them by the drape (a cloth), or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and cut off at both ends, then grind them, and powder over some hot powders that are in the place of cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or fire cautery as said above, or with the paste of cautery, then cure it with other cures until he is well;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, then cauterize the patient with a sharp and bitter caustic to wash what is in the foundation, so that it can come out freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	and if the patient has pain, and his hair comes out easily from the foundation, then the cure is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and are pressed with the nail or tweezers and chopped, then heal them as we have said, until they are well, and fear the incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If it is necessary that you bring the stitch in this way: take a twisted thread and put it into an awl, and then wind the thread over and below the awl, and pierce the awl from the other side, and return the 1.i. 2. threads of the thread through the awl,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide; and pulls the thread tight, then winds the thread, takes out the awl, and does the same to all of them, leaving 1. to stop the blood from flowing;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then put on the foundation 1. cloth soaked in oil or wax, and put it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it until they have finished crying, and when they are calm, if the wounds are treated with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	and then thoroughly dry it at the end or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	For often the drying of the end in the intestines, and by nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then heal him as much as he is sound,
dou fremit	and then heal him as much as he is sound,
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Froge nots of fire comandid on a patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold them steady so they do not move until they are grown.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	For the cure is such that you take a straw from an owl's feather, or a strong vulture's feather, and put that straw on the wound, until the purple circle around the wound is completely gone.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand to all the straw until you cover the entire wound, and put it on properly, and scrub the wound from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, make this of a dog's or iron's shape according to this form, and be subtle and run on top:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	do not pierce, lest it may hurt them both, and must press: And if you see, cauterize the pain, as it is before or with fire of cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the clister
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	No one makes the clister of silver or bronze, or of melted gold or pewter; and no one makes these small or large tools according to these shapes they are brought for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	These are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the small and large enema is over wide, or the belly is tied according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and I have a break or the belly is tied, so that you see it, and the anus is pierced inside; and on one side there is an opening of iij inches, and on the other there is one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly or Om place the medicines in a bladder of best beer or parchment, and pierce all around the smaller openings,
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and place between each hole that there is of space, then pour into these holes a strong thread of twisted rope in ten or twelve times, and wrap around the abdomen so as to form a sheepskin;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, if the instrument has a strong thread in front of it, then cauterize; and this form is that of a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the cauterization with oil or olive oil, or a similar substance, then pour it lightly;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	then spread the minister between his two hands together, until it is completely dry, then remove the cauterization, and place the patient's legs against the wall,
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps a whole night, there is more help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cauterize him with the disease of the belly's decay, and the medicine comes out quickly, continue it until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament or abscess, so be the cautery as subtle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the subtile cautery where the skin is held in place:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already spoken about the treatment of wounds in the division; now we will tell you about the treatment of hands and medicines according to fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are various according to what they are, and according to the places where they are made, and how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that cause wounds are by the fall of a stone, or the size of an spear or a dagger, or a lance or a staff or a sword, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Here is the translation of the text line-by-line into English:
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, beginning with simple head wounds, because the memory comes in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, if it is from falling off a cliff or similar things, and the skin is torn in many places, and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt a little the aposteme: if it comes to heal the cephalic midsommer if it is not poc of blood from the wound, and let the healing be on the opposite side of the wounded part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and prevent the patient from drinking wine and eating large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he cannot urinate, or if his meat is reduced and does not drink wine or eat cheese,
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and apply to the wound, if it is an abscess, cotton dipped in oil and applied coldly, or in wine that constricts.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if it is not an abscess, if it is fresh blood on the wound, and it does not move with air, powder, which I will mention a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it burns him, put it on some herbs, until he is well.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large, like from a sword or similar, and the lips do not come together tightly, then sew them together, like I said for wounds on the belly, by the seam.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	For if the wound is open to the bone and it bleeds profusely, then patch it; but then heal the wound with medicine, and replace the skin with hard leather.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat large meats, like roast beef and bread, as well as birds, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find a boil, and it does not hurt the bone, then cut off the puss, and then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if it has an artery in the wound or vein, which without suturing, and it cannot be stopped by medicine, then cut the artery, and if you find it dislocated, let it be like a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if that does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, then a light cure is given: and that you put this powder which hardens so that the fire moves it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of this powder is this: take Frankincense one part; dragon's blood 16 parts; live coals 13 parts, and the powder finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply the wound, and hold it firm, until it has completely healed and is joined together with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then bind it well, and let it be without a bandage if it swells; for you do not take off the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And never make a fire with only live coals, but if you have only Frankincense and dragon's blood, let the fire not move the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if it has been burned, it moves the wound, most certainly it would be if there was not one of this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but put on some herbs that are digestible, or balls of barley flour made with water and honey, until it no longer has fever;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then he should treat him with other remedies as long as he is healthy.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture of an bone comes with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with gentle pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you hereafter about the breaks of the head.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	The wound comes from the throat and is simple; there is no difference between it and that of the head, but the artery is cut at the throat.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the neck, if there is no other device but to leave the cure alone, and do not put anything that restricts it, for it hurts the neck and makes it retreat;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not put anything on the wound, because the substance of the nerves is cold, and the extension of the blood goes with the brain, which is the most high member;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but be the medicine hot, if as hot water washed down with rose oil, and mixed with oil too, and also washed in hot water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of mine according to this way, and wet with oils.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, so the cost and bind it with bandages, then the cure until he is healed.

et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery has been cut and blood runs, if he faints and falls, and if you cauterize him, your craft is needed.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if his voice from the throat has been cut, or he chokes, and his direction is guarded, so that the meat goes in.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	and if the cut to the curb on the chin of the throat, and does not touch the throat but sets it according to its natural shape;

et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression on the bone, then seek out
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, and the treatment is too painful for you, and these that you cannot bear, leave it until the wound putridity;

et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, sprinkle on the powder I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if it has bones and there is a fistula, then treat it with the ointment as I have said in this chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from a lance or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from a lance or knife, and the wound is deep, then look carefully at the wound to see if there are any signs of life in the patient: know that such wounds are often fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not submerged, and it is fresh in all its blood, then I do not put the powder to it at first hour, nor bind the blood so that it does not hold completely,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and return to the heart, and stop the pain.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I add a soothing remedy, and bind it three times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have ointment, put wet cotton on the wound to absorb the moisture,

et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see the good conditions, if you know that the wound is saved.

et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot be healed, and operated, then know that there is a fistula; so heal as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	and if the wound is from an incision with a knife or sword, and it is simple, or deep or on the back, then heal that which is before;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, of suture; and if it is small, of powder, and if it has pierced the bone, and there are pieces of it, then heal the wound, and if they have been broken, then treat them;
